asoiaf_no_crowns_modifiers = {
    usage = game
	selection_behavior = max
	priority = 3
	
	asoiaf_no_crowns = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = no_headgear
				value = 0
            }
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = secondary_headgear
				template = no_headgear
				value = 0
            }
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = additive_headgear
				template = no_headgear
				value = 0
            }
		}
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = { #unless they have a crown equipped
				add = -5000
				any_equipped_character_artifact = { artifact_slot_type = helmet }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 2000
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_inactive_trait = asoiaf_Hightower_97_trait #Alicent Hightower (daughter of Otto)
						has_game_rule = asoiaf_new_dnas_reach_rule_on
					}
					AND = {
						has_inactive_trait = asoiaf_Hightower_97_trait
						NOT = { this = character:Hightower_97 }
						asoiaf_canon_children_enabled_trigger = yes
						NOT = { has_game_rule = asoiaf_new_dnas_reach_rule_on }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 2000
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_inactive_trait = asoiaf_Velaryon_34_trait #Laena Velaryon (daughter of Corlys)
						has_game_rule = asoiaf_new_dnas_valyrian_rule_on
					}
					AND = {
						has_inactive_trait = asoiaf_Velaryon_34_trait
						NOT = { this = character:Velaryon_34 }
						asoiaf_canon_children_enabled_trigger = yes
						NOT = { has_game_rule = asoiaf_new_dnas_valyrian_rule_on }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 2000
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_inactive_trait = asoiaf_Targaryen_66_trait #Helaena Targaryen (daughter of Viserys I)
						has_game_rule = asoiaf_new_dnas_valyrian_rule_on
					}
					AND = {
						has_inactive_trait = asoiaf_Targaryen_66_trait
						NOT = { this = character:Targaryen_66 }
						asoiaf_canon_children_enabled_trigger = yes
						NOT = { has_game_rule = asoiaf_new_dnas_valyrian_rule_on }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 2000
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_inactive_trait = asoiaf_Lannister_6_trait #Cersei Lannister (daughter of Tywin)
						has_game_rule = asoiaf_new_dnas_westerlands_rule_on
					}
					AND = {
						has_inactive_trait = asoiaf_Lannister_6_trait
						NOT = { this = character:Lannister_6 }
						asoiaf_canon_children_enabled_trigger = yes
						NOT = { has_game_rule = asoiaf_new_dnas_westerlands_rule_on }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
asoiaf_red_priest_necklace_age_modifiers = {
    usage = game
	selection_behavior = max
	priority = 2
	
	asoiaf_red_priest_necklace = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = special_accessories_jewelry
				template = red_priest_necklace_square
				accessory = red_priest_necklace_square_01
            }
		}
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 2500
				any_equipped_character_artifact = { has_variable = asoiaf_red_priest_necklace }
			}
		}
	}
	
	asoiaf_red_priest_necklace_immortality_visuals = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = special_accessories_jewelry
				template = red_priest_necklace_square
				value = 0
            }
			morph = {
				mode = replace
				gene = gene_age
				template = disabled_aging
				value = 1.0
			}
			morph = {
				mode = replace
				gene = gene_baldness
				template = no_baldness
				value = 1.0
			}
			morph = {
				mode = replace
				gene = hair_aging
				template = no_hair_aging
				value = 0.0
			}
			morph = { #stops body from morphing with age, not ideal but all I can do atm
				mode = replace
				gene = gene_bs_body_type
				template = body_average
				value = 0.1
			}
			morph = { #stops brests from morphing with age, not ideal but all I can do atm
				mode = replace
				gene = gene_bs_bust
				template = bust_clothes_light
				value = 0.8
			}
			morph = {
				mode = add
				gene = gene_lovers_pox
				template = none
				value = 0
			}
		}
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 3000
				OR = {
					AND = {
						any_equipped_character_artifact = { has_variable = asoiaf_red_priest_necklace }
						OR = {
							has_trait = lifestyle_mystic
							has_trait = witch
						}
					}
					AND = { #conditions for being a Red Priest
						is_ai = yes
						has_trait = red_priest
						OR = {
							has_trait = witch
							has_trait = lifestyle_mystic
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

asoiaf_priest_clothes_modifiers = {
    usage = game
	selection_behavior = max
	priority = 3
	
	asoiaf_septon_male = { #REGULAR SEPTONS
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = clothes
				template = religious_orthodox_high_clothes
				value = 0
            }
			accessory = {

            }
			#accessory = { #disabled because of the Baelor I exception

				mode = add

				template = no_cloak
				value = 0
            }
		}
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 3000
				AND = {
					has_trait = septon
					is_male = yes
					religion = religion:the_seven_religion
					NOR = { #humble/improvident septons can default to roughspun robes
						has_trait = humble
						has_trait = improvident
					}
					NOT = { should_be_naked_trigger = yes }
					OR = {
						liege.highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						highest_held_title_tier > tier_county #for landed priests
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -3100
				OR = {
					has_trait = nightswatch
					has_trait = kingsguard
				}
			}
		}
	}

asoiaf_misc_dna = {
	usage = game
	asoiaf_kissed_by_fire_modifier_override = { #has a higher weight than vanilla AGOT's, so red priest hair isn't a neon red
		dna_modifiers = {
			color = {
				gene = hair_color
				mode = replace		
				x = 1.0
				y = 0.75
			}
			color = {
				gene = eye_color
				mode = replace
				x = 0.894
				y = 0.2
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify
				gene = gene_height
				range = -0.2 #to undo vanilla AGOT's morphs
			}
        }
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 200 #vanilla is 100
				has_character_flag = portrait_kissed_by_fire
				NOT = { agot_invalid_hair_overrides = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	asoiaf_eye_scar_saphire_gem = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				gene = gene_scars_eye
				template = scars_eye
				range = 1.0
			}
			accessory = { #hidden under the eyepatch, but it's good to know it's there :)
				mode = add
				gene = eye_accessory_gem
				template = one_eyed_gem_saphire
				value = 1.0
            }
        }
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 2000
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_inactive_trait = asoiaf_Targaryen_67_trait #Aemond Targaryen (son of Viserys I)
						has_game_rule = asoiaf_new_dnas_valyrian_rule_on
						has_trait = one_eyed
					}
					AND = {
						has_inactive_trait = asoiaf_Targaryen_67_trait
						has_trait = one_eyed
						asoiaf_canon_children_enabled_trigger = yes
						NOT = { has_game_rule = asoiaf_new_dnas_valyrian_rule_on }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	asoiaf_eye_scar = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				gene = gene_scars_eye
				template = scars_eye
				range = 1.0
			}
        }
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 2000
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_inactive_trait = asoiaf_Targaryen_96_trait #Brynden Rivers (Bloodraven)
						has_game_rule = asoiaf_new_dnas_valyrian_rule_on
						has_trait = one_eyed
					}
					AND = {
						has_inactive_trait = asoiaf_Targaryen_96_trait
						NOT = { this = character:Targaryen_96 }
						asoiaf_canon_children_enabled_trigger = yes
						NOT = { has_game_rule = asoiaf_new_dnas_valyrian_rule_on }
						has_trait = one_eyed
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
